        // Simple micro-interaction for cards
        document.querySelectorAll('.masonry-item').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('touchstart', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(0.98)';
                card.style.transition = 'transform 0.1s ease';
            });
            card.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(1)';

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for quantity selectors
        document.querySelectorAll('.cart-item').forEach(item => {
            const minusBtn = item.querySelector('button:has(span:contains("remove"))');
            const plusBtn = item.querySelector('button:has(span:contains("add"))');
            const countSpan = item.querySelector('span.w-8');
            
            // Note: In real implementation, jQuery-like contains isn't native, 
            // but for this UI demo we'll target by order or classes
        });

        // Toggle All Selection Logic
        const selectAll = document.getElementById('select-all');
        const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.cart-item input[type="checkbox"]');

        selectAll.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => {
                cb.checked = e.target.checked;
            });
        });

        // Add visual feedback to checkboxes
        checkboxes.forEach(cb => {
            cb.addEventListener('change', () => {
                const allChecked = Array.from(checkboxes).every(c => c.checked);
                selectAll.checked = allChecked;
            });
        });
    </script>

        // Simple micro-interaction for adding items to cart
        document.querySelectorAll('button span').forEach(btn => {
            if(btn.innerText === 'add') {
                btn.parentElement.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    const ripple = document.createElement('div');
                    ripple.className = 'absolute inset-0 bg-white/30 rounded-full animate-ping';
                    btn.parentElement.appendChild(ripple);
                    setTimeout(() => ripple.remove(), 500);
                });
            }
        });

<!-- Interactive State Management Script -->
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('button[class*="font-label-md"]');
      
      tabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
          // Reset all tabs
          tabs.forEach(t => {
            t.classList.remove('text-primary-container', 'font-semibold', 'relative');
            t.classList.add('text-on-surface-variant');
            const line = t.querySelector('span');
            if (line) line.remove();
          });

          // Set active tab
          tab.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant');
          tab.classList.add('text-primary-container', 'font-semibold', 'relative');
          
          const activeLine = document.createElement('span');
          activeLine.className = 'absolute -bottom-[17px] left-0 w-full h-[2px] bg-primary-container rounded-full';
          tab.appendChild(activeLine);

          // Simulated filter logic
          const filter = tab.textContent.trim();
          const cards = document.querySelectorAll('article');
          const emptyState = document.getElementById('empty-state');
          let visibleCount = 0;

          cards.forEach(card => {
            const status = card.querySelector('.uppercase')?.textContent.trim() || card.querySelector('.text-outline-variant')?.textContent.trim();
            
            if (filter === 'All') {
              card.classList.remove('hidden');
              visibleCount++;
            } else if (status && status.toLowerCase().includes(filter.toLowerCase().replace('to ', ''))) {
              card.classList.remove('hidden');
              visibleCount++;
            } else {
              card.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          });

          if (visibleCount === 0) {
            emptyState.classList.remove('hidden');
          } else {
            emptyState.classList.add('hidden');
          }
        });
      });
    });
  </script>
</body></html>

<script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('button');
            buttons.forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    const ripple = document.createElement('span');
                    ripple.className = 'absolute bg-white/20 rounded-full scale-0 animate-ping pointer-events-none';
                    ripple.style.width = ripple.style.height = Math.max(this.offsetWidth, this.offsetHeight) + 'px';
                    ripple.style.left = e.offsetX - (parseInt(ripple.style.width)/2) + 'px';
                    ripple.style.top = e.offsetY - (parseInt(ripple.style.height)/2) + 'px';
                    this.style.position = 'relative';
                    this.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                    this.appendChild(ripple);
                    setTimeout(() => ripple.remove(), 600);
                });
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Simple Carousel Logic
        let currentSlide = 0;
        const carousel = document.getElementById('carousel');
        const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.rounded-full');
        
        setInterval(() => {
            currentSlide = (currentSlide + 1) % 3;
            carousel.style.transform = `translateX(-${currentSlide * 33.333}%)`;
            
            // Update dots
            const dotsContainer = carousel.parentElement.querySelector('.bottom-3');
            const dotsArr = Array.from(dotsContainer.children);
            dotsArr.forEach((dot, idx) => {
                if(idx === currentSlide) {
                    dot.className = 'w-4 h-1 bg-[#C9A96E] rounded-full transition-all duration-300';
                } else {
                    dot.className = 'w-1.5 h-1 bg-white/60 rounded-full transition-all duration-300';
                }
            });
        }, 4000);
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for tab switching
        const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('nav div button');
        tabs.forEach(tab => {
            tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
                tabs.forEach(t => {
                    t.classList.remove('text-primary', 'dark:text-primary-fixed-dim', 'font-bold');
                    t.classList.add('text-on-surface-variant', 'dark:text-outline');
                    const indicator = t.querySelector('div');
                    if (indicator) indicator.remove();
                });
                tab.classList.add('text-primary', 'dark:text-primary-fixed-dim', 'font-bold');
                tab.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant', 'dark:text-outline');
                const newIndicator = document.createElement('div');
                newIndicator.className = 'absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 h-0.5 bg-primary dark:bg-primary-fixed';
                tab.appendChild(newIndicator);
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
    document.getElementById('submitOrder').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const btn = this;
      const originalContent = btn.innerHTML;
      
      // Feedback animation
      btn.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined animate-spin">progress_activity</span> Processing...';
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.style.opacity = '0.7';

      setTimeout(() => {
        btn.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined">check_circle</span> ORDER PLACED';
        btn.style.backgroundColor = '#254e3e';
        
        // Success micro-interaction
        const confetti = document.createElement('div');
        confetti.className = 'fixed top-0 left-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-[100]';
        document.body.appendChild(confetti);
        
        // Simple visual confirmation
        setTimeout(() => {
          alert('Thank you for your order! Your premium fruit selection is being prepared.');
          btn.innerHTML = originalContent;
          btn.disabled = false;
          btn.style.opacity = '1';
          btn.style.backgroundColor = '';
        }, 1500);
      }, 2000);
    });

    // Ripple effect for payment options
    const paymentLabels = document.querySelectorAll('label');
    paymentLabels.forEach(label => {
      label.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
        const x = e.clientX - e.target.offsetLeft;
        const y = e.clientY - e.target.offsetTop;
        
        const ripple = document.createElement('span');
        ripple.style.left = `${x}px`;
        ripple.style.top = `${y}px`;
        // Basic interaction logic without heavy CSS
      });
    });
  </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interaction for record cards
        document.querySelectorAll('.bg-surface-container-lowest').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('touchstart', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(0.98)';
                card.style.transition = 'transform 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)';
            });
            card.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
            });
        });

        // Simple visibility observer for lazy-loading feel
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    entry.target.classList.add('opacity-100');
                    entry.target.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'translate-y-4');
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.1 });

        document.querySelectorAll('.bg-surface-container-lowest').forEach(card => {
            card.classList.add('transition-all', 'duration-500', 'opacity-0', 'translate-y-4');
            observer.observe(card);
        });
    </script>
</body></html>

        function openDetails(month) {
            const overlay = document.getElementById('detail-overlay');
            const title = document.getElementById('detail-title');
            title.innerText = month + ' 对账详情';
            overlay.classList.remove('translate-y-full');
        }

        function closeDetails() {
            const overlay = document.getElementById('detail-overlay');
            overlay.classList.add('translate-y-full');
        }
    </script>

<script>
        // Simple micro-interaction for status chips
        const chips = document.querySelectorAll('.scrollbar-hide button');
        chips.forEach(chip => {
            chip.addEventListener('click', () => {
                chips.forEach(c => {
                    c.classList.remove('bg-primary', 'text-on-primary');
                    c.classList.add('bg-surface-container', 'text-on-surface-variant');
                });
                chip.classList.add('bg-primary', 'text-on-primary');
                chip.classList.remove('bg-surface-container', 'text-on-surface-variant');
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        function selectQuality(element) {
            // Reset all chips
            document.querySelectorAll('.quality-chip').forEach(chip => {
                chip.classList.remove('bg-primary-container', 'text-on-primary-container', 'border-primary-container', 'font-bold');
                chip.classList.add('bg-surface-container-lowest', 'text-on-surface-variant', 'border-outline-variant');
            });
            
            // Select clicked chip
            element.classList.remove('bg-surface-container-lowest', 'text-on-surface-variant', 'border-outline-variant');
            element.classList.add('bg-primary-container', 'text-on-primary-container', 'border-primary-container', 'font-bold');
        }

        // Initialize first quality chip
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            selectQuality(document.querySelectorAll('.quality-chip')[0]);
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for tabs
        const supplyTab = document.getElementById('supply-tab');
        const sourcingTab = document.getElementById('sourcing-tab');

        function setActive(active, inactive) {
            active.classList.add('bg-surface-container-lowest', 'text-primary', 'font-bold', 'shadow-sm');
            active.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant', 'opacity-60');
            
            inactive.classList.remove('bg-surface-container-lowest', 'text-primary', 'font-bold', 'shadow-sm');
            inactive.classList.add('text-on-surface-variant', 'opacity-60');
        }

        supplyTab.addEventListener('click', () => setActive(supplyTab, sourcingTab));
        sourcingTab.addEventListener('click', () => setActive(sourcingTab, supplyTab));

        // Background atmosphere: Subtle organic gradient movement
        const bgEffect = document.createElement('div');
        bgEffect.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;z-index:-1;opacity:0.4;background:radial-gradient(circle at 80% 20%, #bfedd7 0%, transparent 40%); pointer-events:none;';
        document.body.appendChild(bgEffect);
    </script>
</body></html>

<script>
        // Form Interaction Logic
        document.getElementById('supplyForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            // Animation for feedback
            const btn = e.target.querySelector('button');
            const originalText = btn.innerText;
            btn.innerText = '正在提交...';
            btn.disabled = true;
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                alert('货源信息发布成功！正在等待经理审核。');
                btn.innerText = originalText;
                btn.disabled = false;
            }, 1500);
        });

        // Add subtle focus effect on container
        const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input, select');
        inputs.forEach(input => {
            input.addEventListener('focus', () => {
                input.closest('.form-card').classList.add('ring-1', 'ring-primary/10');
            });
            input.addEventListener('blur', () => {
                input.closest('.form-card').classList.remove('ring-1', 'ring-primary/10');
            });
        });
    </script>
</body></html>
